Hi
I really wanna give my thoughts on the DLC so far. Ik nobody usually reads my comments and this one is definitely gonna get ignored as usual but I still want to say something but I have nobody to talk about this with. I need to share my thoughts out there, even if no one will listen.. anyways I have pretty mixed feelings about the DLC. There's definitely some good and some bad. It's basically just like the base game all over again. At first I really loved the DLC. It looked super good and felt scary too, I legit got spooked in the beginning even tho it was super obvious. I like the new mechanics of the game, I love the overall feel, and I like Cassie as a character. But then of course there's some disappointments. I really wanted to see more of the Daycare attendant but of course he only appears once and that's it. At least we saw a new side of him which is cool but I wanted to see more of him. Why they gotta do him so dirty? ğŸ˜” I was also kinda hoping we'd see Vanny more because she's such a disappointing antagonist and she really needed more screen time. But of course she wasn't in the DLC at all... can't say I'm surprised. Then we have the endings. Well I'm sure there's at least one more ending left after this but for now, I'm extremely disappointed. It has to be another cliffhanger again and we get more questions than answers. I wasn't really expecting for anything to get answered because let's face it, nothing ever will. FNAF's story will forever remain a mystery. I still hate that we got little to no answers. I wanted to learn more about Gregory and even Cassie. But we got nothing, just more mysteries. I hate how complicated the story has gotten, it's so hard to figure out. I've given up on trying to understand it tbh. I can't do this anymore. I've come to accept that I will never understand it. Ever. So while the DLC wasn't completely disappointing, I'm still upset over some things. Now I'm not sure what we're gonna get next. Will there be another part to the DLC or is that it for Security Breach? This can't be the end, there has to be more. Well I definitely wasted my time typing all of this because I doubt anyone will read this. No one ever seems to pay attention to my comments which always makes me sad... I hope that maybe it will get noticed this time but I doubt it. I guess I'm just talking to the void. Hello void :) Hope you enjoyed my rant. Sorry for the super long comment heheh. It's interesting how from the trailer it seemed like there were things in Ruin that paralleled the Princess Quest games - Chica with conveyor belts, the green & purple colours, the inverted Steelwool logos being like the 2 versions of Cassidy, & the OG Vanny mask.  Now Ruin's released we can see even more parallels to Princess Quest (all of the above plus) imagery of the black glitchy creatures from Princess Quest, the golden sword from the game, the eyes seen through the Vanny mask that appear in cracks in the walls, and imagery of the purple glitchy form of Glitchtrap. However the one thing that hasn't been found yet is the Glitchtrap plushie, which was a key item in Princess Quest. It's interesting that it hasn't been found yet, if included in the game at all and if so I wonder why it would be excluded.
